\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l00900}00900\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ number\ of\ distinct\ groups\ has\ to\ be\ at\ least\ equal\ to\ the\ number\ of\ folds).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l00901}00901\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l00902}00902\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ The\ difference\ between\ :class:\`{}GroupKFold\`{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l00903}00903\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ and\ \`{}StratifiedGroupKFold\`{}\ is\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l00904}00904\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ the\ former\ attempts\ to\ create\ balanced\ folds\ such\ that\ the\ number\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l00905}00905\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ distinct\ groups\ is\ approximately\ the\ same\ in\ each\ fold,\ whereas}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l00906}00906\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}StratifiedGroupKFold\`{}\ attempts\ to\ create\ folds\ which\ preserve\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l00907}00907\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ percentage\ of\ samples\ for\ each\ class\ as\ much\ as\ possible\ given\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l00908}00908\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ constraint\ of\ non-\/overlapping\ groups\ between\ splits.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l00980}00980\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}y\ =\ [1,\ 0]\`{}\`{}\ should\ not\ change\ the\ indices\ generated.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l00983}00983\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ there\ is\ a\ small\ number\ of\ groups\ containing\ a\ large\ number\ of\ samples}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l00984}00984\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ the\ stratification\ will\ not\ be\ possible\ and\ the\ behavior\ will\ be\ close}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l00985}00985\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \ \ to\ GroupKFold.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l02081}02081\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Provides\ randomized\ train/test\ indices\ to\ split\ data\ according\ to\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l02082}02082\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ third-\/party\ provided\ group.\ This\ group\ information\ can\ be\ used\ to\ encode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l02083}02083\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ arbitrary\ domain\ specific\ stratifications\ of\ the\ samples\ as\ integers.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l02086}02086\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ and\ thus\ allow\ for\ cross-\/validation\ against\ time-\/based\ splits.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l02088}02088\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ The\ difference\ between\ :class:\`{}LeavePGroupsOut\`{}\ and\ \`{}\`{}GroupShuffleSplit\`{}\`{}\ is\ that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l02089}02089\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ the\ former\ generates\ splits\ using\ all\ subsets\ of\ size\ \`{}\`{}p\`{}\`{}\ unique\ groups,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l02090}02090\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ whereas\ \`{}\`{}GroupShuffleSplit\`{}\`{}\ generates\ a\ user-\/determined\ number\ of\ random}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l02092}02092\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l02093}02093\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ For\ example,\ a\ less\ computationally\ intensive\ alternative\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l02094}02094\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}LeavePGroupsOut(p=10)\`{}\`{}\ would\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l02095}02095\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}GroupShuffleSplit(test\_size=10,\ n\_splits=100)\`{}\`{}.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l02097}02097\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ Contrary\ to\ other\ cross-\/validation\ strategies,\ the\ random\ splits}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{__split_8py_source_l02098}02098\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\ \ \ \ do\ not\ guarantee\ that\ test\ sets\ across\ all\ folds\ will\ be\ mutually\ exclusive,}}
